function paru_demo

%
% Usage: paru_demo
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_many, paru_tiny, mldivide.

% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.

type paru_demo
load west0479
A = west0479 ;
n = size (A,1) ;
b = rand (n,1) ;
x = A\b ;
norm (A*x-b)
x2 = paru (A,b) ;
norm (A*x2-b)

paru_demo

function paru_demo
%PARU_DEMO: test a single sparse matrix in ParU
%
% Usage: paru_demo
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_many, paru_tiny, mldivide.

% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.
% SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later

type paru_demo
load west0479
A = west0479 ;
n = size (A,1) ;
b = rand (n,1) ;
x = A\b ;
norm (A*x-b)
x2 = paru (A,b) ;
norm (A*x2-b)


ans =

   1.2686e-10

malloc 0x7eff6d4ea0e0 0x7eff6c0b8840 NOW

ans =

   1.5002e-09
